<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a> (72853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lively, quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snellaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">active, swift, brisk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">active, strenuous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></i> (whence German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schnell.html>schnell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, swift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">שנעל</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">shnel</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, swift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">snello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">esnel, isnel</i> <span class="mention-gloss">clever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneller.html>sneller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">snellest</b>)
</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Quick, smart; sharp, active, brisk or nimble; lively.
<ul><li><b>1720</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Allan Ramsay, <i>Edinburgh's Salutation to Lord Carnarvon</i>.
<dl><dd>That in ilk action, wise and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> / You may shaw Manly fire.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1852</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> John Brown, "<a href = vnd.unilang:rab.html>Rab</a> and his Friends".
<dl><dd>That horny-handed, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b>, peremptory little <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1889</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> James Robertson, <i>The Early Religion of Israel</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:amos.html>Amos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lithe, keen, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Quick-witted; witty.</li>
<li>Harsh; severe.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">snells</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A short line of horsehair, gut, <a href = vnd.unilang:monofilament.html>monofilament</a>, etc., by which a fishhook or lure <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attached to a longer (and usually heavier) line.
<ul><li><b>1979</b>, Cormac McCarthy, <i>Suttree</i>, Random House, p.194:
<dl><dd>He tied on new baited <b>snells</b> and recovered the current with the oars.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">snells</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snelling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snelled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To tie a hook to the end of a fishing line with a <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a> knot.
<dl><dd><i>Can you show <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> how to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> a hook?</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***snicker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a> (88079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>US variant of the British <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snigger</i>, possibly of imitative origin, similar to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snikken.html>snikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gasp; sob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> first recorded 1836, from the verb. Compare also Scottish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">smicker</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile or laugh in a sniggering or <a href = vnd.unilang:leery.html>leery</a> way, smirk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smicker</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A stifled or broken laugh.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snickering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snickered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To emit a <a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a>, a stifled or broken laugh.
<ul><li><b>1915</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/T.S._Eliot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:T.S. Eliot"><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>.S. Eliot</a>, "The Love Song of J. Alfred Prufrock":
<dl><dd>I have seen the eternal Footman hold my coat, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></b> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To utter through a laugh of this <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a horse</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To whinny.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:laugh</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snick</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A player who snicks the ball.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a> (34677)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***snijboon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboon</a> (67426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, named because they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> usually cut into small pieces before cooking or eating.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijbonen.html>snijbonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> bean</span>, a long variety of <i>Phaseolus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>, with <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> pods and fully matured seeds.</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Phaseolus_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Phaseolus vulgaris"><span style="color:green;"><i>Phaseolus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plantensoort.html>plantensoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brede.html>brede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:platte.html>platte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:peulen.html>peulen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesneden.html>gesneden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegeten.html>gegeten</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sniden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">snīthan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snīþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sneyt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snic</i>. ***snikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snikken.html>snikken</a> (34676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sob; gasp for breath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Probably related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiven.html>snuiven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> under the influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snakken.html>snakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to open the mouth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hik.html>hik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hiccup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">snucken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">snokke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Norwegian dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">snukka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, German dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnuckeln</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnauken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnäuken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff; sob forcefully</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snip</a> (99670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snippe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snippen.html>snippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snipje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A snipe or <a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a>, thin-beaked bird of the genera <i>Gallinago</i>, <i>Scolopax</i>, <i>Lymnocryptes</i>, <i>Limnodromus</i> and <i>Coenocorypha</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A 100 guilders banknote.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snode.html>snode</a> (22101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snōthi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snauþijaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">snôde</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>poor, needy</li>
<li>paltry, of little value</li>
<li>bad, worthless</li>
<li>low in standing</li>
<li>lowly, despised</li>
<li>miserable, pitiful</li></ol>

***snood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snood.html>snood</a> (112918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snôde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snōthi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snauþuz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bald, naked, poor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ksnéw-tu-s</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ksnew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scrape, sharpen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnöde</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">snauðr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snood.html>snood</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snood.html>snoder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">snoodst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>villanous and criminal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekokstoven.html>bekokstoofde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snood.html>snood</a></b> plan.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He concocted a <b>villainous</b> plan.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***snor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a> (4747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">snorbaard</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">snurbaard</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Snurrbaart</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Snurboart</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schnurrbart</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorren.html>snorren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorretje.html>snorretje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>moustache</li></ol>

***snorhaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snorhaar.html>snorhaar</a> (62957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorhaar.html>snorhaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorharen.html>snorharen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorhaar.html>snorhaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A whisker of certain non-human mammals, such as those of <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>cats</a> and rodents.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A moustache hair; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> moustache hair.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snorkel.html>snorkel</a> (50690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in the 1949. Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorkel.html>snorkel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schnorchel</i>. The German word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined in the 1940s to describe the Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiver.html>snuiver</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snorkel.html>snorkel</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">swimming gear, breathing tube</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snotte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snotto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snuttuz</i>.

***snowball.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a> (50689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">snoweball</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">snoweballe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">snaweballe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">snayballe</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snow</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ball</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">snawbaw</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schneeball</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Schnéiball</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwbal.html>sneeuwbal</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">sneeubal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">snieëbal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sniebal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Sneebaal</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Sneebal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">snöboll</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elfdalian" class="extiw" title="w:Elfdalian">Elfdalian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ovd">sniųoboll</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">snebold</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nb">snøball</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nynorsk" class="extiw" title="w:Nynorsk">Norwegian Nynorsk</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">snøball</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">snjóbolti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ball of snow, usually one made in the hand and thrown for amusement in a <a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a> fight; also a larger ball of snow made by rolling a <a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a> around in snow that <a href = vnd.unilang:sticks.html>sticks</a> to it and increases its diameter.</li>
<li>A cocktail made from lemonade and <a href = vnd.unilang:advocaat.html>advocaat</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something that <a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a> (grows rapidly out of control).
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, Eldad Ben-Yosef, <i>The Evolution of the US Airline Industry</i>
<dl><dd>Representatives of the small airlines that felt betrayed by Brown's policy started a political <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a></b> rolling, resulting in the Airmail Act of 1934...</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A sex act involving passing ejaculated semen from one person's mouth to another's.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A type of ice <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a>.</li>
<li>A type of cake. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snowball.html>snowball</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snowballing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snowballed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rapidly grow out of proportion or control.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The high unemployment rates quickly <b>snowballed</b> into a major budget problem for the government.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2020</b> May 6,  Philip Haigh,  “Just one more <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> on the long journey to HS2 fulfillment <span style="font-style: normal;">[</span>sic<span style="font-style: normal;">]</span>”, in  <cite>Rail</cite>, page 65:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Operating the WCML at this intensity <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> it challenging to maintain acceptable performance levels, resulting in a frustratingly unreliable service for passengers. Minor disruption can escalate into significant delays because a train running only a few minutes late can miss its <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> across a junction, resulting in a <b>snowballing</b> effect across the network."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To play at throwing <a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pelt with <a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a>; to throw <a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a> at.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>sexual <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></i>) To receive a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s ejaculate in one's mouth, and then to pass it back and forth between one's mouth and his.</li></ol>
</body>

***snowman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a> (19117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snow</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-man</i>. A <a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a> (when built from two <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>) resembles an 8.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">snowmen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A humanoid figure made with large <a href = vnd.unilang:snowballs.html>snowballs</a> stacked on each other. Human traits like a face and arms may be fashioned with <a href = vnd.unilang:sticks.html>sticks</a> (arms), a carrot (nose), and stones or coal (<a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>, mouth).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball<span class="ib-comma">,</span> golf</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A score of eight, especially within one inning (in baseball) or on one hole (in golf, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also known as dogballs).
<ul><li><b>1996</b> June 3, <a href = vnd.unilang:buster.html>Buster</a> Olney, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.baltimoresun.com/news/bs-xpm-1996-06-03-1996155019-story.html">Chat with <a href = vnd.unilang:sparky.html>Sparky</a> helps 'useless' Johnson   Dejected <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'s manager <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a> from Ex-Tigers boss</a>", in <i>The Baltimore Sun</i>, quoting B. J. Surhoff:
<dl><dd>"[The Angels] dropped a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a></b> early on us [Saturday] and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> built a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a></b> early too."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b> June 26, <i>Dayton Daily News</i> (44):
<dl><dd>"Then they dropped a <a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a> (8) on us and <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> it pretty quick," Narron <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>. "Then Stone <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to stay out there and suck it up for us <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2018</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:andre.html>Andre</a> Huu, <i>The Round of Your Life: A Book on Golf and Life</i>, Archway Publishing (→ISBN):
<dl><dd>For <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, another blow-up score of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>snowman</a></b>, 8, seems about right on this hole.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A playing card with the rank of eight.</li>
<li>An attractive but heartless <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> (similar to ice queen).
<ul><li><b>1961</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_D._Loudermilk" class="extiw" title="w:John D. Loudermilk">John D. Loudermilk</a> in the song "The Great <a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>Snowman</a>"
<dl><dd>A few years ago there lived a lover By the name of <a href = vnd.unilang:jimmy.html>Jimmy</a> Jones Who really snowed the <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a> and left them cold And gained the title of 'The Great <a href = vnd.unilang:snowman.html>Snowman</a>'.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***snuf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snuf.html>snuf</a> (79499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuf.html>snuffen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to snuff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuf.html>snuf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuf.html>snuffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snufje.html>snufje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>smell, odor</li>
<li>snuff, sniffle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Its diminutive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snufje.html>snufje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> some additional independent meanings.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snuut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snūt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snūtaz</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snuiter.html>snuiter</a> (18915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiter.html>snuiter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiter.html>snuiters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiter.html>snuitertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>snuffer
<ol><li>type of scissors used for extinguishing candles</li>
<li>conical extinguisher</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (curious) fellow, chap, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a strange chap</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>When denoting a person, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very often preceded by the pleonastic epithets <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raar.html>raar</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vreemd.html>vreemd</a></i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiter.html>snuiter</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snuiven.html>snuiven</a> (12591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snuyven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snūvan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snūbaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe, puff, blow, snort</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, imitative of drawing air through the nose, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">snūfen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnauben</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiven.html>snuiven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiver.html>snuiver</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuivers.html>snuivers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiver.html>snuivertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
